	<script type="text/javascript">
		var pageURL = window.location.href;
		var siteCode = "sec";

		var digitalData = {
			"page" : {
				"pageInfo" : {
					"siteCode" : siteCode
					, "siteSection" : ""
					, "pageName" : ""
					, "pageURL" : pageURL
					, "pageTrack" : "product search"
					, "version" : "KDP"
				}
				, "pathIndicator" : {
					"depth_2" : ""
					, "depth_3" : ""
					, "depth_4" : ""
					, "depth_5" : ""
				}
			}
			, "user" : {
				"loginStatus" : ""
			}
			, "product" : {
				"category" : ""
				, "model_code" : ""
				, "model_name" : ""
				, "displayName" : ""
				, "pvi_type_code" : ""
				, "pvi_type_name" : ""
				, "pvi_subtype_code" : ""
				, "pvi_subtype_name" : ""

			}
		}

		// depth Info.
		var depth = window.location.href.split("/").length;
		var depth_last = window.location.href.split("/")[depth-1];
		if(depth_last =="" || depth_last.charAt(0)=="?"){
			depth -= 1;
		}

		// set site section value
		if((digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2 != "")||(digitalData.page.pageInfo.pageTrack == "flagship pdp")){
			if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2 == "shop" || digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2 == "my account"){
				digitalData.page.pageInfo.siteSection = siteCode + ":" + digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2;
			}else{
				digitalData.page.pageInfo.siteSection = siteCode + ":consumer"; //product page
			}
		}else if(depth == 4){
			digitalData.page.pageInfo.siteSection = siteCode + ":home"; //home
		}else{
			digitalData.page.pageInfo.siteSection = siteCode + ":" + window.location.href.split("/")[4];
		}

		// set product category value
		/* 	if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_3 != ""){
	    digitalData.product.category = digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_3;
	} */

		// set pathIndicator(not product page)
		if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2 == ""){
			if(depth >= 5) digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2 = window.location.href.split("/")[4].toLowerCase();
			if(depth >= 6) digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_3 = window.location.href.split("/")[5].toLowerCase();
			if(depth >= 7) digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_4 = window.location.href.split("/")[6].toLowerCase();
			if(depth >= 8) digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_5 = window.location.href.split("/")[7].toLowerCase();
		}

		// set pageName
		var pageName = siteCode;
		if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2 != "")
			pageName += ":" + digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_2;
		if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_3 != "")
			pageName += ":" + digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_3;
		if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_4 != "")
			pageName += ":" + digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_4;
		if(digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_5 != "")
			pageName += ":" + digitalData.page.pathIndicator.depth_5.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/gm,'');

		// check PD, GPD
		var pageTrackName = digitalData.page.pageInfo.pageTrack;
		if(pageTrackName == "product detail" || pageTrackName == "generic product details"){
			pageName += ":" + digitalData.product.model_code;
			var displayName = "".replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/gi, "");
			digitalData.product.displayName = displayName;
		}
		digitalData.page.pageInfo.pageName = pageName;

	</script>

		var searchResultManager = {
			isJsonString: function(str) {
				try {
					var json = JSON.parse(str);
					return (typeof json === 'object');
				} catch (e) {
					return false;
				}
			},
			callAjax: function(options) {
				waiting.start();
				jQuery.ajaxSettings.traditional = true;

				options.contentType = options.contentType == undefined ? "application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=UTF-8" : options.contentType;
				options.type        = setDefaultIfNull(options.type, "POST");
				options.dataType    = setDefaultIfNull(options.dataType, "json");
				options.async       = (options.async == null || options.async) ? true : false;
				options.beforeSend  == undefined ? undefined : options.beforeSend;
				options.processData = options.processData == undefined ? true: options.processData;

				$.ajax({
					url         : options.url,
					type        : options.type,
					dataType    : options.dataType,
					contentType : options.contentType,
					data        : options.data,
					async       : options.async,
					beforeSend  : options.beforeSend,
					processData : options.processData

				}).done(function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
					if ( searchResultManager.isJsonString(data) ) {
						data = JSON.parse(data);
					}

					if (data.exCode != null && data.exCode !== "") {
						if (options.fail !== undefined) {
							options.fail();
						}
						let alertData = {
							title: "alert",
							content: data.exMsg
						};
						commonAlert(alertData);
						openLayer('commonAlert');
					} else {
						options.done(data);
						waiting.stop();
					}
				}).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
					waiting.stop();

					if (options.fail !== undefined) {
						options.fail();
					}
					if (jqXHR.status !== 0) {
						ajax.error(jqXHR.status, jqXHR.responseText);
					}
				}).always(function(data) {
					waiting.stop();
				}).then(function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
				});
			},
			callAjaxWithoutDim: function(options) {
				$.ajax({
					url : options.url,
					type: options.type,
					data: options.data

				}).done(function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
					if (data.exCode != null && data.exCode !== "") {
						if (options.fail !== undefined) {
							options.fail();
						}
						let alertData = {
							title: "alert",
							content: data.exMsg
						};
						commonAlert(alertData);
						openLayer('commonAlert');
					} else {
						options.done(data);
					}
				}).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
					if (options.fail !== undefined) {
						options.fail();
					}
					if (jqXHR.status !== 0) {
						ajax.error(jqXHR.status, jqXHR.responseText);
					}
				}).always(function() {
				}).then(function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
				});
			},
			/* 모바일 여부 확인 */
			isMobileDevice: function() {
				var that = this,
						winW = $(window).width();
				if ( winW > 800 ) {
					return 'N';
				} else {
					return 'Y';
				}
			},

			/* s: Url query parameter 확인 */
			getQueryParam: function(){
				var url = document.location.href;
				var qs  = url.substring(url.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');

				for(var i = 0, result = {}; i < qs.length; i++){
					qs[i] = qs[i].split('=');
					result[qs[i][0]] = decodeURIComponent(qs[i][1]);
				}
				return result;
			},
			/* e: Url query parameter 확인 */

			/* s: Tab 초기화 */

			// 모든 조건 초기화
			initCondition: function() {
				var that = searchResultManager;

				that.currentCollection       = undefined; // 현재 collection
				that.minPrice                = '';
				that.maxPrice                = '';
				that.isSliderClicked         = false;
				that.isSliderClickedForEvent = false;
				that.isNeededInitializing    = true;
				that.isFilterSet             = undefined;
				that.filterQueryList         = undefined;
				that.isFilterSet             = undefined;
			},
			/* e: Tab 초기화 */

			/* s: Tab 클릭 */
			// Tab 클릭(고객서비스, 디지털프라자 제외)
			initTab: function(collectionName) {
				var that       = searchResultManager
						, currentUrl = location.href;

				// URL로 값이 들어오지 않은 경우
				if ( !that.isTabTriggered ) {
					currentUrl = (location.href).replace(/(.*?keyword=.*?)|(\&)(.*)/gi, '$1').replace(/(.*searchresult\/)(.*?)(\?.*)/gi, '$1' + collectionName + '/$3')
					history.pushState(null, null, currentUrl);
				}

				that.initCondition();
				that.initFilter(collectionName);

				that.$filterAppendingTarget = $('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .filter-cont');

				// URL로 값이 들어온 경우
				if ( that.isTabTriggered ) {
					that.initResultWhenTabTriggered(collectionName);

				} else {
					$('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]').attr('page', '0');
					$($('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li')[0]).trigger('click');
				}

				$('html').scrollTop(0);
				that.isTabTriggered = undefined;
			},

			// Tab 클릭(고객서비스, 디지털프라자)
			initFixedSubTabContents: function(elementId, that) {
				var $triggerTarget    = $(elementId + ' div[role=tablist] div.tab-list a')
						, tabType           = $(that).attr('tab-type')
						, queryParam        = searchResultManager.getQueryParam()
						, currentCollection = queryParam.currentCollection;

				if ( $triggerTarget.length > 0 ) {
					if ( searchResultManager.isTabTriggered ) {
						if ( currentCollection == undefined ) {
							$($triggerTarget[0]).trigger('click');
							searchResultManager.isTabTriggered = undefined;
							return;

						} else {
							$.each($triggerTarget, function(idx, element) {
								if ( $(element).attr('collection-name') == currentCollection ) {
									$(element).trigger('click');
									searchResultManager.isTabTriggered = undefined;
									return;
								}
							});
						}
						if ( searchResultManager.isTabTriggered ) {
							$($triggerTarget[0]).trigger('click');
						}

						return;
					}
					$($triggerTarget[0]).trigger('click');
				}
			},

			// Tab 클릭(고객서비스, 디지털프라자의 하위 category)
			initTabSub: function(collectionName) {
				var that              = searchResultManager
						, topCollectionName = searchConstants[collectionName].TAB_NAME;

				that.initCondition();
				that.initFilter(collectionName);
				that.currentCollection = collectionName;

				// URL로 값이 들어온 경우
				if ( that.isTabTriggered ) {
					that.initResultWhenTabTriggered(collectionName);

				} else {
					$('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]').attr('page', '0');
					currentUrl = (location.href).replace(/(.*?keyword=.*?)|(\&)(.*)/gi, '$1').replace(/(.*searchresult\/)(.*?)(\?.*)/gi, '$1' + topCollectionName + '/$3')
					history.pushState(null, null, currentUrl);

					$($('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + topCollectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li')[0]).trigger('click');
				}

				$('html').scrollTop(0);
				that.isTabTriggered    = undefined;
				that.topCollectionName = undefined;
			},
			/* s: Tab 클릭 */

			/* s: URL에 값이 설정되어 들어온 경우 */
			initResultWhenTabTriggered: function(collectionName) {
				var that                   = searchResultManager
						, $btnMobileContentsMore = $('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
						, isSliderClicked        = that.isSliderClicked
						, queryParam             = that.getQueryParam()
						, currentPage            = queryParam.currentPage
						, sort                   = queryParam.sort
						, exQuery                = queryParam.exQuery
						, minPrice               = queryParam.minPrice
						, maxPrice               = queryParam.maxPrice
						, isMobileYN             = that.isMobileDevice()
						, isBestMatchYn          = queryParam.isBestMatchYn
						, suggestion             = queryParam.suggestion
						, incl                   = queryParam.incl
						, excl                   = queryParam.excl
						, pageSize               = queryParam.pageSize
						, isFilterSet            = 'N'
						, isFilter1stSet         = 'Y'
						, data                   = ''
						, searchConstant         = searchConstants[collectionName]
						, constant               = searchConstant['TAB']
						, paginationHtml         = constant.paginationHtml
						, searchParamPageSize	   = constant.PAGESIZE; // 20200921 추가

				if ( isMobileYN == 'Y') {
					that.isNeededInitializing = undefined;
					that.isFilterSelected     = undefined;
					that.callback             = that.mobileCallback;

				} else {
					that.callback = that.pcCallback;
				}

				that.pageNum                 = currentPage;
				that.searchConstant          = searchConstant;
				that.isFilterSet             = undefined;
				that.isFilter1stSet          = isFilter1stSet;
				that.isSliderClickedForEvent = false;

				$btnMobileContentsMore.attr('page', that.pageNum);
				$btnMobileContentsMore.show();

				that.setResearchKeywordQueryParam(incl, excl);

				// 20200921 추가
				if( collectionName == 'event' && isMobileYN == 'Y') {
					searchParamPageSize = that.searchConstant['TAB'].MOBILE_PAGESIZE;
				}

				// exQuery가 없는 경우
				if ( exQuery == undefined || exQuery == '') {

// 							data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE, '', ''
// 									, '', '', '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
// 									, isFilterSet, isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet, '', currentPage, 'Y', incl, excl);
					// 20200921 수정
					data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, searchParamPageSize, '', ''
							, '', '', '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
							, isFilterSet, isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet, '', currentPage, 'Y', incl, excl);

					that.getTabContents(sort, data);
					that.setConditionsByQueryParam(data);
					return;
				}

				// exQuery가 있는 경우

// 						data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), pager.getStartCount(), that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE, '', ''
// 									, maxPrice, minPrice, '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', isMobileYN, isBestMatchYn, suggestion
// 									, isFilterSet, isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet, '' , currentPage, 'Y', incl, excl);
				// 20200921 수정
				data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), pager.getStartCount(), that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, searchParamPageSize, '', ''
						, maxPrice, minPrice, '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', isMobileYN, isBestMatchYn, suggestion
						, isFilterSet, isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet, '' , currentPage, 'Y', incl, excl);


				// pager init
				pager.init({
					data                 : data,
					pageSize             : data.pageSize,
					initialize           : true,
					blockSize            : 5,
					pagingHtml           : '<li><a href="javascript:;"></a></li>',
					appendingTargetHtml  : constant.appendingTarget,
					paginationHtml       : paginationHtml,
					paginationTargetHtml : paginationHtml + ' ul',
					paginationWingBarHtml: paginationHtml + ' span',
					firstBtnClass        : ' .btn_first',
					prevBtnClass         : ' .btn_prev',
					nextBtnClass         : ' .btn_next',
					lastBtnClass         : ' .btn_last',
					callback             : that.callback
				});

				pager.currentPage        = currentPage;
				pager.data.isBestMatchYn = that.isBestMatchYn;
				pager.data.exQuery       = exQuery;
				pager.data.sort          = sort;
				pager.data.minPrice      = minPrice;
				pager.data.maxPrice      = maxPrice;
				pager.data.startCount    = pager.getStartCount();

				that.initFilterTabContents(data);
			},

			// 데이터 호출 ajax
			initFilterTabContents: function(data) {
				var that = searchResultManager;
				that.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/getSearchContentsByTab/',
					data        : data,
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						that.commonInitFilterTabContentsCallback(false, result, data);
					}
				});
			},

			// 데이터 호출 ajax callback
			commonInitFilterTabContentsCallback: function(isMobile, result, data) {
				var $result               = $(result)
						, that                  = searchResultManager
						, collectionName        = data.collection
						, $list                 = $result.find('#list').children()
						, $filterList           = $result.find('#filterList')
						, $flexibleFilterList   = $result.find('#flexibleFilterList')
						, $flexibleInFilterList = $filterList.find('#flexible')
						, $fixedInFilterList    = $filterList.find('#fixed').children()
						, $priceInFilterList    = $filterList.find('#price').children()
						, $filterAppendingList  = that.$filterAppendingTarget
						, count                 = $result.find('#count').text()
						, isBestMatchYn         = $result.find('#isBestMatchYn').children()
						, old_scroll            = $(window).scrollTop();

				$(pager.appendingTargetHtml).empty();
				$(pager.appendingTargetHtml).append($list);

				if ( count == '' ) {
					count = 0;
				}

				// 필터 적용결과 count 수정
				$('div.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .result-num span.num').text(count);

				pager.data.isTriggeredByTab = undefined;
				pager.totalCount            = count;
				pager.initialize            = true;
				pager.isPagingDataSet       = false;
				pager.getPage(pager.currentPage);

				// 제품 이외의 Tab
				if ( collectionName != 'product' ) {
					$filterAppendingList.prepend($filterList.children());
					that.setConditionsByQueryParam(data);
					that.isFilterSet = 'Y';
					return;
				}

				// 제품 Tab
				var isBestMatchYn      = $result.find('#isBestMatchYn').text()
						, $selectedFilterDiv = $filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable[selected="selected"]');

				// 1. 카테고리 설정
				$filterAppendingList.append($fixedInFilterList);
				that.isFilterSet = 'Y';

				// 2. 하위 유형 및 고정 filter 설정
				$filterAppendingList.append($flexibleInFilterList.children());
				$filterAppendingList.find('.first-item').after($flexibleFilterList.children());

				// 3. 가격 설정
				$filterAppendingList.append($priceInFilterList);
				that.minPrice = data.minPrice;
				that.maxPrice = data.maxPrice;
				searchApp.priceRange();

				$('.price-slider div.cont').on('mouseup', that.eventListener.filterPriceMouseDown);
				$('span.ui-slider-handle').on('mousedown', function() {
					that.isSliderClicked         = true;
					that.isSliderClickedForEvent = true;
				});
				$('div.price-range.ui-slider').on('mousedown', function() {
					that.isSliderClicked         = true;
					that.isSliderClickedForEvent = true;
				});

				searchResultManager.isBestMatchYn = isBestMatchYn;
				pager.data.isBestMatchYn = isBestMatchYn;

				if ( that.isMobileDevice() == 'Y' ) {
					if ( pager.lastPage == pager.currentPage ) {
						$('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]').hide();
					}
					$(document).scrollTop(old_scroll);
				}

				that.setConditionsByQueryParam(data);
			},
			// query param에 따른 조건 설정
			setConditionsByQueryParam: function(data) {
				var that           = searchResultManager
						, collectionName = data.collection
						, $dropList      = $('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"]')
						, sort           = data.sort
						, $currentSortLi = $dropList.find('li[sort="' + sort + '"]')
						, sortName       = $currentSortLi.text()
						, exQuery        = data.exQuery
						, rekeyword      = data.rekeyword
						, $filterBtn     = $('.sort-control button[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
						, $btnReset      = $('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .btn-filter-reset');

				// sort 설정
				that.setSortingConditionsByQueryParam(collectionName, sort);

				if ( exQuery == undefined || exQuery == '' ) {
					return;
				}

				that.isFilterSelected = true;

				// filter 설정(exQuery가 있는 경우)
				// collection이 product가 아닌 경우
				if ( collectionName != 'product' ) {
					var $filterList      = that.getFilterQueryList(collectionName, exQuery)
							, $filterWrap      = $('div.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
							, $filterInput     = $filterWrap.find('div.filter-cont ul li input')
							, is1DepthSelected = false
							, is2DepthSelected = false;

					$.each($filterInput, function(idx, element) {
						$.each($filterList, function(idx2, element2) {
							var $element                = $(element)
									, $filterUl               = $element.parent().parent()
									, filterType              = $filterUl.attr('filter-type')
									, filterName              = $filterUl.attr('filter-name')
									, $filterDiv              = $('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName +'"]')
									, filterValue             = $element.attr('code')
									, $appendingTarget        = ''
									, appendingText           = $element.next().text()
									, filterValue             = $element.attr('code')

							if ( filterValue == element2 ) {
								$element.attr('selected', 'selected');
								$element.prop('checked', true);
								$appendingTarget = $(that.eventListener.filterAppendingHtml(filterType, filterValue, appendingText, 'changeable'));
								that.setFilterQuery(element2);

								$appendingTarget.on('click', 'button.btn-delete', function(e) {
									that.eventListener.deleteBtnFilter(e, collectionName);
								});

								$('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] ul').append($appendingTarget);
							}
						});
					});

					// collection이 product인 경우
				} else {
					var $filterList      = that.getFilterQueryList(collectionName, exQuery)
							, $filterWrap      = $('div.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
							, $filterInput     = $filterWrap.find('div.filter-cont ul li input')
							, $filterBtn       = $('.sort-control button[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
							, is1DepthSelected = false
							, is2DepthSelected = false;

					$.each($filterInput, function(idx, element) {
						$.each($filterList, function(idx2, element2) {
							var $element                = $(element)
									, $filterUl               = $element.parent().parent()
									, filterType              = $filterUl.attr('filter-type')
									, filterName              = $filterUl.attr('filter-name')
									, $filterDiv              = $('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName +'"]')
									, filterValue             = $element.attr('code')
									, $appendingTarget        = ''
									, appendingText           = $element.next().text()
									, filterValue             = $element.attr('code')
									, filterText              = filterName + ':' + filterValue
									, $filterDiv              = $('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName +'"]');

							if ( filterText == element2 ) {
								$filterDiv.attr('selected', 'selected');
								$element.attr('selected', 'selected');
								$element.prop('checked', true);

								var key       = ''
										, classType = '';

								// 카테고리 Depth1
								if ( filterType == 'category') {
									key              = searchConstants.filter.product.CATEGORY_L;
									classType        = 'fixed';
									is1DepthSelected = true;
									$('.filter-cont .category-depth2 li[code="' + filterValue + '"]').show();

									// 카테고리 Depth2
								} else if ( filterType == 'check' ) {
									key              = searchConstants.filter.product.CATEGORY_M;
									classType        = 'fixed';
									is2DepthSelected = true;

									// 그 이외 filter
								} else {
									key       = filterName;
									classType = 'changeable';
								}

								$appendingTarget = $(that.eventListener.filterAppendingHtml(filterType, filterValue, appendingText, classType));
								that.setFilterProductQuery(key, filterText);

								$appendingTarget.on('click', 'button.btn-delete', function(e) {
									that.eventListener.deleteProductBtnFilter(e);
								});

								$('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] ul').append($appendingTarget);
							}
						});
					});

					if ( is1DepthSelected ) {
						$('.filter-cont .category-depth2').show();
					}
					if ( is2DepthSelected ) {
						$('.filter-cont .flexible-filter-item li').show();
						$('.filter-cont .flexible-filter-item').show();
					}
				}

				$btnReset.removeAttr('disabled');
				$filterBtn.trigger('click');
			},
			// 정렬 조건 설정
			setSortingConditionsByQueryParam: function(collectionName, sort) {
				// 해당하는 정렬이 없는지 체크
				if ( sort == undefined || sort == ''
						|| !(sort == searchConstants.sort.RELEVANCE
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.PRICE_DESC
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.PRICE_ASC
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.TITLE_DESC
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.TITLE_ASC
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.LATEST
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.OLDEST
								|| sort == searchConstants.sort.POPULARITY)) {
					return;
				}

				var that              = searchResultManager
						, topCollectionName = that.topCollectionName;

				// 고객서비스, 디지털프라자인 경우
				if ( topCollectionName != undefined && topCollectionName != '' ) {
					collectionName = topCollectionName;
				}

				var $dropList      = $('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"]')
						, $currentSortLi = $dropList.find('li[sort="' + sort + '"]')
						, sortName       = $currentSortLi.text();

				$dropList.removeAttr('aria-selected');
				$dropList.removeClass('focused');
				$dropList.prev().text(sortName);
				$currentSortLi.addClass('focused');
				$currentSortLi.attr('aria-selected', 'selected');
			},
			/* e: URL에 값이 설정되어 들어온 경우 */

			/* s: Tab 데이터 호출 */
			// 데이터 호출 ajax : PC / Mobile
			getTabContents: function(sort, data) {
				var that           = searchResultManager
						, constant       = that.searchConstant['TAB']
						, paginationHtml = constant.paginationHtml
						, sort           = sort == undefined ? '' : sort
						, pageNum        = that.pageNum == undefined? 1 : that.pageNum;

				pager = new Pager();
				pager.init({
					data                 : data,
					pageSize             : data.pageSize,
					initialize           : true,
					blockSize            : 5,
					totalCount           : that.searchConstant.TOTAL_COUNT,
					pagingHtml           : '<li><a href="javascript:;"></a></li>',
					appendingTargetHtml  : constant.appendingTarget,
					paginationHtml       : paginationHtml,
					paginationTargetHtml : paginationHtml + ' ul',
					paginationWingBarHtml: paginationHtml + ' span',
					firstBtnClass        : ' .btn_first',
					prevBtnClass         : ' .btn_prev',
					nextBtnClass         : ' .btn_next',
					lastBtnClass         : ' .btn_last',
					callback             : that.callback
				});

				pager.currentPage           = pageNum;
				pager.data.startCount       = pager.getStartCount();
				pager.callAjax();
				pager.data.isTriggeredByTab = undefined;
				pager.getPage(pageNum);
			},

			// PC 데이터 호출
			pcCallback: function() {
				var that = this;

				that.data.currentPage = pager.currentPage;

				searchResultManager.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/getSearchContentsByTab/',
					data        : that.data,
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						var $result = $(result)
								, $list   = $result.find('#list').children();

						$(that.appendingTargetHtml).empty();
						$(that.appendingTargetHtml).append($list);

						searchResultManager.commonFilterCallback($result, that.data);
					}
				});
			},

			// Mobile 데이터 호출
			mobileCallback: function() {
				var that        = this
						, currentPage = searchResultManager.pageNum;

				that.currentPage = currentPage == undefined ? 1 : currentPage;
				that.data.startCount = that.getStartCount();
				that.data.currentPage = pager.currentPage;

				searchResultManager.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/getSearchContentsByTab/',
					data        : that.data,
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						var $result    = $(result)
								, $list      = $result.find('#list').children()
								, old_scroll = $(window).scrollTop();

						if ( searchResultManager.isNeededInitializing || searchResultManager.isFilterSelected ) {
							$(pager.appendingTargetHtml).empty();
						}

						$(that.appendingTargetHtml).append($list);
						searchResultManager.commonFilterCallback($result, that.data);
						$(document).scrollTop(old_scroll);
					}
				});
			},

			// PC / Mobile 공통 callback
			commonFilterCallback: function($result, data) {
				var that                  = searchResultManager
						, collectionName        = data.collection
						, $filterList           = $result.find('#filterList')
						, $fixedInFilterList    = $filterList.find('#fixed').children()
						, $flexibleInFilterList = $filterList.find('#flexible').children()
						, $priceInFilterList    = $filterList.find('#price').children()
						, $filterAppendingList  = that.$filterAppendingTarget
						, isFilterSet           = that.isFilterSet
						, count                 = $result.find('#count').text();

				pager.data.isTriggeredByTab = undefined;
				that.setCurrentUrl(that.getCurrentUrlByParam(data, pager));

				if ( count == '' ) {
					count = 0;
				}
				$('div.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .result-num span.num').text(count);

				// 1. colleciton이 product가 아닌 경우
				if ( collectionName != 'product' ) {
					if ( isFilterSet == undefined && $filterAppendingList != undefined ) {
						$filterAppendingList.prepend($filterList.children());
						that.isFilterSet = 'Y';
					}
					return;
				}

				// 2. colleciton이 product인 경우
				// 처음 데이터가 setting된 경우가 아니면 filter를 변경하지 않음
				if ( pager.isPagingDataSet ) {
					return;
				}

				$filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable').remove();
				if ( isFilterSet == undefined && $filterAppendingList != undefined ) {
					$filterAppendingList.prepend($fixedInFilterList);
					that.isFilterSet = 'Y';
				}
				$filterAppendingList.append($flexibleInFilterList);

				// 가격이 변동된 경우만 가격 slider 설정(paging에서 선택된 가격 slider는 유지)
				if ( !searchResultManager.isSliderClicked ) {
					$filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable-price').remove();
					$filterAppendingList.append($priceInFilterList);
					that.minPrice = $priceInFilterList.find('span.min-range').text();
					that.maxPrice = $priceInFilterList.find('span.max-range').text();
					searchApp.priceRange();

					$('.price-slider div.cont').on('mouseup', that.eventListener.filterPriceMouseDown);
					$('span.ui-slider-handle').on('mousedown', function() {
						that.isSliderClicked         = true;
						that.isSliderClickedForEvent = true;
					});
					$('div.price-range.ui-slider').on('mousedown', function() {
						that.isSliderClicked         = true;
						that.isSliderClickedForEvent = true;
					});
				}
			},
			/* e: Tab 데이터 호출 */

			/* s: 정렬 데이터 조회 */
			// 전체 Tab 정렬(고객서비스, 디지털프라자 제외)
			getAllSortedContents: function(sort) {
				var that                  = searchResultManager
						, constant              = that.searchConstant['ALL']
						, collectionName        = that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME
						, isProductSearchAllTab = 'N'
						, isMobileYN			  = that.isMobileDevice() // 20200921 추가
						, searchParamPageSize   = constant.PAGESIZE; // 20200921 추가

				if( collectionName == 'event' && isMobileYN == 'Y') { // 20200921 추가
					searchParamPageSize = constant.MOBILE_PAGESIZE;
				}

				sort == undefined ? '' : sort;

				if ( collectionName == searchConstants.product.COLLECTION_NAME ) {
					isProductSearchAllTab = 'Y';
				}

				searchResultManager.callAjax({ // 20200921 data의 WNSearchParamVo 수정
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/getSearchContentsByTab/',
					data        : new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, collectionName
							, sort, searchParamPageSize, '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
							, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet, isProductSearchAllTab),
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						var $result = $(result)
								, $list   = $result.find('#list').children();

						$(constant.appendingTarget).empty();
						$(constant.appendingTarget).append($list);
					}
				});
			},
			// 전체 Tab 정렬(고객서비스, 디지털프라자)
			getAllSortedMultiContents: function(collectionName, sort, callback) {
				var that     = searchResultManager
						, constant = that.searchConstant['ALL'];

				sort == undefined ? '' : sort;

				searchResultManager.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/searchmultiresult/',
					data        : new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, collectionName, sort
							, '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
							, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet),
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						callback(result);
					}
				});
			},

			// PC filter 설정된 경우 데이터 조회
			getFilterTabContents: function(data) {
				var that = searchResultManager;
				that.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/getSearchContentsByTab/',
					data        : data,
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						that.commonFilterTabContentsCallback(false, result, data);
					}
				});
			},

			// Mobile filter 설정된 경우 데이터 조회
			getFilterMobileTabContents: function(data) {
				var that = searchResultManager;
				that.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/getSearchContentsByTab/',
					data        : data,
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						that.commonFilterTabContentsCallback(true, result, data);
					}
				});
			},
			// PC, Mobile 공통 Callback
			commonFilterTabContentsCallback: function(isMobile, result, data) {
				var $result               = $(result)
						, that                  = searchResultManager
						, collectionName        = data.collection
						, $list                 = $result.find('#list').children()
						, $filterList           = $result.find('#filterList')
						, $fixedInFilterList    = $filterList.find('#fixed').children()
						, $priceInFilterList    = $filterList.find('#price').children()
						, $filterAppendingList  = that.$filterAppendingTarget
						, count                 = $result.find('#count').text()
						, isBestMatchYn         = $result.find('#isBestMatchYn').children()
						, old_scroll            = $(window).scrollTop();

				$(pager.appendingTargetHtml).empty();
				$(pager.appendingTargetHtml).append($list);

				if ( count == '' ) {
					count = 0;
				}

				// 필터 적용결과 count 수정
				$('div.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .result-num span.num').text(count);

				pager.totalCount      = count;
				pager.initialize      = true;
				pager.isPagingDataSet = false;
				pager.getPage(1);

				that.setCurrentUrl(that.getCurrentUrlByParam(data, pager));

				if ( collectionName == 'product' ) {
					var isBestMatchYn      = $result.find('#isBestMatchYn').text()
							, $selectedFilterDiv = $filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable[selected="selected"]');

					// filter 설정
					$filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable').not('[selected="selected"]').remove();

					if ( that.isFilter1stSet == 'Y' ) {
						var $flexibleFilterList = $result.find('#flexibleFilterList');

						$.each($selectedFilterDiv, function(idx, element) {
							var filterName = $(element).attr('filter-name');
							$flexibleFilterList.find('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName + '"]').remove();
						});

						var flexibleFilterLast = $filterAppendingList.find('.flexible-filter-item').last();
						if ( flexibleFilterLast == undefined || flexibleFilterLast.length == 0 ) {
							$filterAppendingList.find('.first-item').after($flexibleFilterList.children());

						} else {
							flexibleFilterLast.after($flexibleFilterList.children());
						}

						$filterAppendingList.find('.flexible-filter-item').show();
					}

					// 가격 설정(가격을 선택하지 않은 경우만)
					if ( !that.isSliderClicked ) {
						$filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable-price').remove();
						$filterAppendingList.append($priceInFilterList);

						that.minPrice = $priceInFilterList.find('span.min-range').text();
						that.maxPrice = $priceInFilterList.find('span.max-range').text();
						that.eventListener.initPriceSlider();

						$('.price-slider div.cont').on('mouseup', that.eventListener.filterPriceMouseDown);
						$('span.ui-slider-handle').on('mousedown', function() {
							that.isSliderClicked         = true;
							that.isSliderClickedForEvent = true;
						});
						$('div.price-range.ui-slider').on('mousedown', function() {
							that.isSliderClicked         = true;
							that.isSliderClickedForEvent = true;
						});
					}

					var $flexibleInFilterList = $filterList.find('#flexible');
					$.each($selectedFilterDiv, function(idx, element) {
						var filterName = $(element).attr('filter-name');
						$flexibleInFilterList.find('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName + '"]').remove();
					});

					$filterAppendingList.find('div.changeable-price').before($flexibleInFilterList.children());

					searchResultManager.isBestMatchYn = isBestMatchYn;
					pager.data.isBestMatchYn = isBestMatchYn;
				}

				if ( that.isMobileDevice() == 'Y' ) {
					if ( pager.lastPage == pager.currentPage ) {
						$('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + pager.collectionName + '"]').hide();
					}
					$(document).scrollTop(old_scroll);
				}
			},
			/* e: 정렬 데이터 조회 */

			/* s: 재검색(포함, 제외 검색어) */
			// 재검색 검색어 포함한 검색어
			getKeyword: function() {
				var that = searchResultManager;

				if ( that.reKeyword != undefined) {
					return that.keyword + that.reKeyword;
				}

				return that.keyword;
			},
			// 재검색 데이터 조회
			reSearchResult: function(reKeyword) {
				reKeyword = reKeyword.trim();
				if ( reKeyword == '' ) {
					commonAlert({
						content : '검색어를 입력해주세요.'
					});
					openLayer('commonAlert');
					return;
				}

				var that                = searchResultManager
						, searchType          = $('#research-form input:checked').attr('id')
						, keyword             = that.keyword
						, $keywordList        = $('.keyword-list')
						, $keywordListWrapper = $('.result-tit.searchbar-item');

				if ( that.reKeyword == undefined ) {
					that.reKeyword = '';
				}

				// '포함'인 경우
				if ( searchType == 'radioReSearch1' ) {
					if ( that.includeKeywords == undefined ) {
						that.includeKeywords = [];
					}
					if ( that.excludeKeywords != undefined ) {
						var idx = -1;
						for (var i = 0; i < that.excludeKeywords.length; ++i) {
							if (that.excludeKeywords[i] == reKeyword) {
								idx = i;
								break;
							}
						}
						if ( idx > -1 ) {
							that.excludeKeywords.splice(idx, 1);
						}
					}
					if ( $.inArray(reKeyword, that.includeKeywords) < 0) {
						that.includeKeywords.push(reKeyword);
					}

					// '제외'인 경우
				} else if ( searchType == 'radioReSearch2' ) {
					if ( that.excludeKeywords == undefined ) {
						that.excludeKeywords = [];
					}
					if ( that.includeKeywords != undefined ) {
						var idx = -1;
						for (var i = 0; i < that.includeKeywords.length; ++i) {
							if (that.includeKeywords[i] == reKeyword) {
								idx = i;
								break;
							}
						}
						if ( idx > -1 ) {
							that.includeKeywords.splice(idx, 1);
						}
					}
					if ( $.inArray(reKeyword, that.excludeKeywords) < 0) {
						that.excludeKeywords.push(reKeyword);
					}
				}
				that.setReSearchText();
				$keywordList.show();

				if ( !$keywordListWrapper.hasClass('type-keyword') ) {
					$keywordListWrapper.addClass('type-keyword');
				}
				$('#tabAll').trigger('click');
				that.searchAllCallback(new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, '', '', '', '', ''
						, '', '', '', '', '', '', 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
						, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet), that.keyword);
			},
			// 재검색 데이터 설정(상위 재검색 keyword 목록)
			setReSearchText: function() {
				var that         = searchResultManager
						, $keywordList = $('.keyword-list')
						, reKeywordText = '';

				$keywordList.empty();
				$.each(that.includeKeywords, function(idx, keyword) {
					reKeywordText += ' ' + keyword;
					$keywordList.append('<span class="type-include">\'' + keyword + '\'</span>');
				});

				$.each(that.excludeKeywords, function(idx, keyword) {
					reKeywordText += '!(' + keyword + ')';
					$keywordList.append('<span class="type-except">\'' + keyword + '\'</span>');
				});

				that.reKeyword = reKeywordText;
			},
			// 재검색 결과 없는 경우 결과 화면의 재검색 keyword 설정
			getResearchTextInResult: function() {
				var that         = searchResultManager
						, reKeywordHtml = '';

				$.each(that.includeKeywords, function(idx, keyword) {
					reKeywordHtml += '<b class="type-include">\'' + keyword + '\'</b>';
				});

				$.each(that.excludeKeywords, function(idx, keyword) {
					reKeywordHtml += '<b class="type-except">\'' + keyword + '\'</b>';
				});

				return reKeywordHtml;
			},
			// 데이터 조회 ajax
			searchAllCallback: function(data, keyword) {
				var that = searchResultManager;

				that.callAjax({
					url         : '/sec/xhr/search/searchallresult/?keyword=' + encodeURIComponent(keyword),
					data        : data,
					method      : 'POST',
					dataType    : 'text',
					contentType : 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
					done        : function(result) {
						var $result      = $(result)
								, $contentsAll = $result.find('#contentsAll').children()
								, totalCount   = $result.find('#totalCount').text();

						$('.result-tab-box').empty();
						$('.search-result-wrap').empty();

						$('.searchbar-item span.search-count').text(totalCount);
						$('span.result-num-txt span.num').text(totalCount);
						$('.filter-summary span.num').text(totalCount);

						that.setCurrentUrlWithResearchText();

						if ( totalCount == 0 ) {
							$($contentsAll.find('#noResultText')).prepend(that.getResearchTextInResult());
							$('div.unified-search-inner div.search-result-wrap').append($contentsAll);

						} else {
							var $tabList           = $result.find('#tabList').children()
									, isBestMatchYn      = $result.find('#isBestMatchYn').text()
									, $countTab          = $result.find('#countTab')
									, productCount       = $countTab.find('#product').text()
									, reviewCount        = $countTab.find('#review').text()
									, eventCount         = $countTab.find('#event').text()
									, storyCount         = $countTab.find('#story').text()
									, companyCount       = $countTab.find('#company').text()
									, manualCount        = $countTab.find('#serviceManual').text()
									, newsCount          = $countTab.find('#serviceNotice').text()
									, appServiceCount    = $countTab.find('#serviceAppService').text()
									, plazaEventCount    = $countTab.find('#digitalEvent').text()
									, plazaBaseCount     = $countTab.find('#digitalBase').text()
									, communityCount     = $countTab.find('#community').text()
									, $serviceFirstChild = $($('#serviceTabList a')[0])
									, $plazaFirstChild   = $($('#digitalPlazaTabList a')[0]);

							$('.result-tab-box').append($tabList);
							$('.search-result-wrap').append($contentsAll);

							if ( $serviceFirstChild != undefined ) {
								$serviceFirstChild.attr('aria-selected', 'true');
							}
							if ( $plazaFirstChild != undefined ) {
								$plazaFirstChild.attr('aria-selected', 'true');
							}

							searchConstants.product.TOTAL_COUNT           = productCount;
							searchConstants.review.TOTAL_COUNT            = reviewCount;
							searchConstants.event.TOTAL_COUNT             = eventCount;
							searchConstants.story.TOTAL_COUNT             = storyCount;
							searchConstants.company_info.TOTAL_COUNT      = companyCount;
							searchConstants.serviceManual.TOTAL_COUNT     = manualCount;
							searchConstants.serviceNotice.TOTAL_COUNT     = newsCount;
							searchConstants.serviceAppService.TOTAL_COUNT = appServiceCount;
							searchConstants.digitalEvent.TOTAL_COUNT      = plazaEventCount;
							searchConstants.digitalBase.TOTAL_COUNT       = plazaBaseCount;
							searchConstants.community.TOTAL_COUNT         = communityCount;

							that.isBestMatchYn = isBestMatchYn;
							that.eventListener.initResearchEventListener();
						}
					}
				});
			},
			// URL에 값이 설정되어 들어온 경우
			getResearchKeyword: function(list) {
				var rearchText = '';

				$.each(list, function(idx, element) {
					rearchText += '%2B' + element;
				});

				return rearchText;
			},
			/* e: 재검색 */

			/* s: 오탈자 무시 검색 */
			getSearchResultNoSuggestion: function(keyword) {
				searchInputManager.saveSearchHistory(keyword);
				window.location.href = '/sec/search/searchresult/?keyword=' + encodeURIComponent(keyword) + '&sug=N';
			},
			/* e: 오탈자 무시 검색 */

			/* s: URL data 설정 */
			// 현재 설정된 값을 query param으로 생성
			getCurrentUrlByParam: function(data, pager, sug) {
				var that           = searchResultManager
						, queryParamText = ''
						, queryParamData = {
					sort              : data.sort,
					pageSize          : data.pageSize,
					maxPrice          : data.maxPrice,
					minPrice          : data.minPrice,
					exQuery           : data.exQuery,
					useMobileYN       : data.useMobileYN,
					isBestMatchYn     : data.isBestMatchYn,
					useSuggestQueryYN : data.useSuggestQueryYN,
					incl              : that.getResearchKeyword(that.includeKeywords),
					excl              : that.getResearchKeyword(that.excludeKeywords)
				}
						, pagerParamData = {
					currentPage : pager.currentPage
				}
						, currentCollection = that.currentCollection;

				if ( currentCollection != '' && currentCollection != undefined ) {
					queryParamData.currentCollection = currentCollection;
				}

				if ( sug != '' && sug != undefined ) {
					queryParamData.sug = sug;
				}

				$.each(queryParamData, function(idx, element) {
					var currentUrlByParamText = that.getCurrentUrlByParamText(idx, element);
					if ( !(currentUrlByParamText == '' || currentUrlByParamText == undefined)) {
						queryParamText += '&' + currentUrlByParamText;
					}
				});

				if ( pagerParamData != undefined ) {
					$.each(pagerParamData, function(idx, element) {
						var currentUrlByParamText = that.getCurrentUrlByParamText(idx, element);
						if ( !(currentUrlByParamText == '' || currentUrlByParamText == undefined)) {
							queryParamText += '&' + currentUrlByParamText;
						}
					});
				}

				return queryParamText;
			},

			getCurrentUrlByParamText: function(key, value) {
				if ( key != undefined && key != ''
						&& value != undefined && value != '') {
					return key + '=' + value;
				}
			},

			// URL에 현재 data의 query param 설정
			setCurrentUrl: function(queryParam) {
				var currentUrl     = (location.href).replace(/(.*?keyword=.*?)|(\&)(.*)/gi, '$1')
						, regExp         = /(.*?)(exQuery=.*?)(\&.*)|$/g
						, regExpExQuery  = /^exQuery/g
						, queryParamList = regExp.exec(queryParam)
						, queryParamText = '';

				if( queryParamList != undefined && queryParamList != '' ) {
					$.each(queryParamList, function(idx, element) {
						if ( idx != 0 && element != undefined && element != '' ){
							if ( regExpExQuery.exec(element) != null ) {
								queryParamText += element.replace(/\+/g, '%2B').replace(/\|/g, '%7C');
							} else {
								queryParamText += element;
							}
						}
					});
				}

				if ( queryParamText == '' ) {
					queryParamText = queryParam;
				}
				history.pushState(null, null, currentUrl + queryParamText);
			},

			// 재검색 시 URL 설정
			setCurrentUrlWithResearchText: function() {
				var that       = searchResultManager
						, incl       = that.getResearchKeyword(that.includeKeywords)
						, excl       = that.getResearchKeyword(that.excludeKeywords)
						, currentUrl = (location.href).replace(/(.*?keyword=.*?)|(\&)(.*)/gi, '$1').replace(/(.*searchresult\/).*?(\?.*)/gi, '$1$2') + '&sug=N';

				if( incl != undefined && incl != '' ) {
					currentUrl += '&incl=' + incl;
				}

				if( excl != undefined && excl != '' ) {
					currentUrl += '&excl=' + excl;
				}

				history.pushState(null, null, currentUrl);
			},

			// 재검색 query param 설정
			setResearchKeywordQueryParam: function(inclText, exclText) {
				var that         = searchResultManager
						, regExp       = /(%2B)([가-힣a-zA-Z0-9\s]*)*/g
						, includeList  = that.includeKeywords
						, excludeList  = that.excludeKeywords
						, researchList;

				if ( inclText != undefined ) {
					inclText = inclText.replace(/\+/g, '%2B');

					if ( includeList == undefined ) {
						includeList = [];
					}
					while( researchList = regExp.exec(inclText) ) {
						includeList.push(researchList[2]);
					}
					that.includeKeywords = includeList;
				}

				if ( exclText != undefined ) {
					exclText = exclText.replace(/\+/g, '%2B');

					if ( excludeList == undefined ) {
						excludeList = [];
					}

					while( researchList = regExp.exec(exclText) ) {
						excludeList.push(researchList[2]);
					}
					that.excludeKeywords = excludeList;
				}

				var $keywordList        = $('.keyword-list')
						, $keywordListWrapper = $('.result-tit.searchbar-item');

				that.setReSearchText();
				$keywordList.show();

				if ( !$keywordListWrapper.hasClass('type-keyword') ) {
					$keywordListWrapper.addClass('type-keyword');
				}
			},
			/* e: URL data 설정 */

			/* s: filter */
			// 해당 collection의 filter 초기화
			initFilter: function(collectionName) {
				var that       = searchResultManager
						, $btnReset  = $('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .btn-filter-reset')
						, $filterBtn = $('.sort-control button[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]');

				if ( $filterBtn.hasClass('is-active') ) {
					$filterBtn.trigger('click');
				}
				that.eventListener.initFilterByCategory();

				$btnReset.attr('disabled', 'disabled');
				$('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] ul').empty();
				$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] input:checked').prop('checked', false);
				$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] ul input').removeAttr('selected');
				$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] .filter-cont').empty();
				$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.changeable').removeAttr('selected');

				that.filterQueryList  = undefined;
				that.isFilterSet      = undefined;
				that.isFilter1stSet   = undefined;
				that.isFilterSelected = undefined;

				pager.data = {};
			},

			// 모든 filter 초기화
			initAllFilter: function() {
				var that       = searchResultManager
						, $btnReset  = $('.filter-footer .btn-filter-reset')
						, $filterBtn = $('.sort-control button');

				if ( $filterBtn.hasClass('is-active') ) {
					$filterBtn.trigger('click');
				}
				$btnReset.attr('disabled', 'disabled');
				$('.filter-footer ul').empty();
				$('.result-filter-wrap input:checked').prop('checked', false);
				$('.result-filter-wrap ul input').removeAttr('selected');

				that.eventListener.initPriceSlider();
				that.filterQueryList  = undefined;
				that.isFilterSet      = undefined;
				that.isFilter1stSet   = undefined;
				that.isFilterSelected = undefined;
			},

			// 선택된 filter 데이터 설정 (collection이 product가 아닌 경우)
			setFilterQuery: function(filterText) {
				var that            = searchResultManager
						, filterQueryList = that.filterQueryList;

				if ( filterQueryList == undefined ) {
					filterQueryList = [];
				}

				filterQueryList.push(filterText);
				that.filterQueryList = filterQueryList;
			},

			// 선택된 filter 데이터 설정 (collection이 product인 경우)
			setFilterProductQuery: function(key, filterText) {
				var that               = searchResultManager
						, filterProductQuery = that.filterProductQuery;

				if ( filterProductQuery == undefined ) {
					filterProductQuery = {};
				}

				var filterProductQueryList = filterProductQuery[key];
				if ( filterProductQueryList == undefined) {
					filterProductQueryList = [];
				}

				filterProductQueryList.push(filterText);
				filterProductQuery[key] = filterProductQueryList;
				that.filterProductQuery = filterProductQuery;
			},

			// exQuery 생성 (collection이 product가 아닌 경우)
			getFilterQuery: function(filterKey) {
				var delimiter           = '%7C'
						, that            = searchResultManager
						, filterQueryList = that.filterQueryList
						, filterQuery     = '';

				if ( filterQueryList == undefined ) {
					return '';
				}

				$.each(filterQueryList, function(idx, element) {
					filterQuery += element;

					if ( idx < filterQueryList.length - 1 ) {
						filterQuery += delimiter;
					}
				});

				return filterQuery.trim();
			},

			// exQuery 생성 (collection이 product인 경우)
			getFilterProductQuery: function() {
				var and                   = '%2B'
						, or                    = '%7C'
						, that                  = searchResultManager
						, filterProductQuery    = that.filterProductQuery
						, newFilterProductQuery = {}
						, filterQuery           = '';

				if ( filterProductQuery == undefined ) {
					return '';
				}

				var totalLength = 0;
				$.each(filterProductQuery, function(idx, filterQueryList) {
					if ( filterQueryList.length > 0 ) {
						newFilterProductQuery[idx] = filterQueryList;
						totalLength ++;
					}
				});

				var i = 0;
				$.each(newFilterProductQuery, function(idx, filterQueryList) {
					var filterQuerySub = '';

					$.each(filterQueryList, function(idx2, element) {
						filterQuerySub += element;

						if ( idx2 < filterQueryList.length - 1 ) {
							filterQuerySub += or;
						}
					});
					filterQuery += filterQuerySub;
					if ( i < totalLength - 1 ) {
						filterQuery += and;
					}

					i ++;
				});

				return filterQuery.trim();
			},

			// exQuery 목록 생성
			getFilterQueryList: function(collectionName, exQuery) {
				exQuery = exQuery.replace(/\+/gi, '%2B').replace(/\|/gi, '%7C');

				var regExp = ''
						, exQueryList = ''
						, filterQueryList = [];

				if ( collectionName == 'product' ) {
					regExp = /(.*?):(.*?)(\%2B|\%7C|$)+/g;

					while( exQueryList = regExp.exec(exQuery) ) {
						filterQueryList.push(exQueryList[1] + ':' + exQueryList[2]);
					}

				} else {
					regExp = /(.*?\w+)(%7C|$)*/g;

					while( exQueryList = regExp.exec(exQuery) ) {
						filterQueryList.push(exQueryList[1]);
					}
				}

				return filterQueryList;
			},

			// exQuery text 생성
			getFilterText: function(filterKey, filterValue) {
				return '{' + filterKey + ':contains:' + filterValue + '}';
			},

			// 필터 삭제(collection이 product가 아닌 경우)
			removeFilterQuery: function(filterText) {
				var that            = searchResultManager
						, filterQueryList = that.filterQueryList;

				var idx = -1;
				for (var i = 0; i < filterQueryList.length; ++i) {
					if (filterQueryList[i] == filterText) {
						idx = i;
						break;
					}
				}
				if ( idx > -1 ) {
					filterQueryList.splice(idx, 1);
					that.filterQueryList = filterQueryList;
				}
			},

			// 필터 삭제(collection이 product인 경우)
			removeFilterProductQuery: function(key, filterText) {
				var that                   = searchResultManager
						, filterProductQuery     = that.filterProductQuery
						, filterProductQueryList = filterProductQuery[key];

				var idx = -1;
				for (var i = 0; i < filterProductQueryList.length; ++i) {
					if (filterProductQueryList[i] == filterText) {
						idx = i;
						break;
					}
				}

				if ( idx > -1 ) {
					filterProductQueryList.splice(idx, 1);
					that.filterProductQuery[key] = filterProductQueryList;
				}

			},

			// collection이 product인 경우 해당 key 이외의 filter 모두 삭제
			removeFilterProductQueryByKey: function(key1, key2) {
				var that                  = searchResultManager
						, filterProductQuery    = that.filterProductQuery
						, newFilterProductQuery = {};

				$.each(filterProductQuery, function(idx, element) {
					if ( idx == key1 || idx == key2 ) {
						newFilterProductQuery[idx] = element;
					}
				});

				that.filterProductQuery = newFilterProductQuery;
			},
			/* e: filter */

			getContentsUrlByStContextPath: function(link) {
				var contextPath         = '/sec/'
						, replacedContextPath = contextPath.replace(/\//g, '')
						, regExp = new RegExp('(.*?\/' + replacedContextPath + '\/)|(http.*?:\/\/.(.*?)(\/)|(\/' + replacedContextPath + '\/))|(^\/)');

				window.location.href = contextPath + link.replace(regExp, '');
			},

			eventListener: {
				/* s: dropdown list 이벤트 */
				dropDownList: function(e) {
					e.preventDefault();
					var $dropWrap = $(this).parent();
					var $dropList = $(this).next();
					var dropListBtm;
					var docHeight = $(document).innerHeight();
					if(!$dropWrap.hasClass("nodrop")){          // 클래스 nodrop이 없는 엘리먼트에만 이벤트 적용
						if (!$dropWrap.hasClass("active")) {
							$dropWrap.addClass("active");
							$dropList.find(">li").each(function(){
								$(this).attr("tabindex", -1);
							});

							if ( $dropList.length > 0 ) {
								dropListBtm = $dropList.outerHeight() + $dropList.offset().top;
								if(docHeight < dropListBtm){
									$dropWrap.addClass("bottom");
								}
							}

							$(this).attr("aria-expanded", "true");
							$dropList.focus();
							$dropList.find("[aria-selected]").focus();
						} else {
							$dropWrap.removeClass("active").removeClass("bottom");
							$(this).removeAttr("aria-expanded").focus();
						}
					}
				},
				/* e: dropdown list 이벤트 */

				/* s: Tab 정렬 이벤트 */
				// PC 정렬변경 시 데이터 조회(고객서비스, 디지털프라자 제외)
				sortingTabResult: function(e) {
					var $target        = $(e.target)
							, that           = searchResultManager
							, sort           = $target.attr('sort')
							, $ul            = $target.closest('ul')
							, collectionName = $ul.attr('collection-name')
							, $droplist      = $('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li[aria-selected="selected"]')
							, currentSort    = $droplist.attr('sort');

					if ( that.isMobileYN == 'Y' ) {
						if ( currentSort != sort ) {
							that.isNeededInitializing = true;
						}
						that.eventListener.getSortingMobileResult(0, collectionName, sort);

					} else {
						that.eventListener.getSortingResult(collectionName, sort);
					}
				},
				// PC 정렬변경 시 데이터 조회(고객서비스, 디지털프라자)
				sortingSubTabResult: function(e) {
					var $target           = $(e.target)
							, that              = searchResultManager
							, sort              = $target.attr('sort')
							, $ul               = $target.closest('ul')
							, currentCollection = that.currentCollection
							, $droplist         = $('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + currentCollection + '"][search-type="TAB"] li[aria-selected="selected"]')
							, currentSort       = $droplist.attr('sort');

					if ( that.isMobileYN == 'Y' ) {
						if ( currentSort != sort ) {
							that.isNeededInitializing = true;
						}
						that.eventListener.getSortingMobileResult(0, currentCollection, sort);

					} else {
						that.eventListener.getSortingResult(currentCollection, sort);
					}

				},
				// Mobile 정렬변경 시 데이터 조회(고객서비스, 디지털프라자 제외)
				sortingMobileTabResult: function(e) {
					var $target        = $(e.target)
							, that           = searchResultManager
							, currentSort    = $target.attr('sort')
							, pageNum        = $target.attr('page')
							, collectionName = $target.attr('collection-name')
							, $droplist      = $('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li[aria-selected="selected"]')
							, sort           = $droplist.attr('sort');

					that.isFilterSelected = undefined;
					that.eventListener.getSortingMobileResult(pageNum, collectionName, sort);
				},
				// Mobile 정렬변경 시 데이터 조회(고객서비스, 디지털프라자)
				sortingMobileSubTabResult: function(e) {
					var $target        = $(e.target)
							, that           = searchResultManager
							, pageNum        = $target.attr('page')
							, collectionName = $target.attr('collection-name')
							, sort           = $('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + searchConstants[collectionName].TAB_NAME + '"][search-type="TAB"] li[aria-selected="selected"]').attr('sort');

					that.isFilterSelected = undefined;
					that.isNeededInitializing = undefined;
					that.eventListener.getSortingMobileResult(pageNum, collectionName, sort);
				},

				// PC Tab 데이터 조회
				getSortingResult: function(collectionName, sort) {
					var that = searchResultManager
							, $btnMobileContentsMore = $('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
							, isSliderClicked = that.isSliderClicked;

					that.callback       = that.pcCallback;
					that.pageNum        = 1;
					that.searchConstant = searchConstants[collectionName];

					$btnMobileContentsMore.attr('page', that.pageNum);
					$btnMobileContentsMore.show();

					var data     = ''
							, exQuery  =  '';

					if ( collectionName == 'product' ) {
						exQuery = that.getFilterProductQuery();

					} else {
						exQuery = that.getFilterQuery(searchConstants.filter.FILTER_CATEGORY);
					}

					if ( (exQuery == undefined || exQuery == '') && !isSliderClicked ) {
						that.getTabContents(
								sort,
								new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE, '', ''
										, '', '', '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
										, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet));

						return;
					}

					var minPrice = searchResultManager.minPrice
							, maxPrice = searchResultManager.maxPrice;

					if ( !searchResultManager.isSliderClicked ) {
						minPrice = '';
						maxPrice = '';
					}

					data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE, '', ''
							, maxPrice, minPrice, '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
							, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet);

					pager.data.isBestMatchYn = that.isBestMatchYn;
					pager.data.exQuery       = exQuery;
					pager.data.sort          = sort;
					pager.data.minPrice      = minPrice;
					pager.data.maxPrice      = maxPrice;
					pager.data.startCount    = pager.getStartCount();

					that.getFilterTabContents(data);
				},

				// Mobile Tab 데이터 조회
				getSortingMobileResult: function(pageNum, collectionName, sort) {
					var that                   = searchResultManager
							, currentPage            = parseInt(pageNum) + 1
							, $btnMobileContentsMore = $('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"]')
							, isSliderClicked        = that.isSliderClicked;


					that.callback       = that.mobileCallback;
					that.pageNum        = currentPage;
					that.collectionName = collectionName;
					that.searchConstant = searchConstants[collectionName];

					var searchParamPageSize = that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE; // 20200921 추가

					if( collectionName == 'event') { // 20200921 추가
						searchParamPageSize = that.searchConstant['TAB'].MOBILE_PAGESIZE;
					}

					$btnMobileContentsMore.attr('page', currentPage);
					$btnMobileContentsMore.show();

					var data     = ''
							, exQuery  = '';

					if ( collectionName == 'product' ) {
						exQuery = that.getFilterProductQuery();
					} else {
						exQuery = that.getFilterQuery(searchConstants.filter.FILTER_CATEGORY);
					}

					// Paging 처리)
					if ( currentPage > 1 ) {
						that.isNeededInitializing = undefined;

						pager.isPagingDataSet = true;
						pager.getPage(currentPage);
						pager.callAjax();
						if ( pager.lastPage == pager.currentPage ) {
							$('.mo-contents-more a[collection-name="' + searchResultManager.collectionName + '"]').hide();
						}

						return;
					}

					// 처음 조회하는 경우
					if ( (exQuery == undefined || exQuery == '') && !isSliderClicked ) {

// 								data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE, '', ''
// 										, '', '', '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
// 										, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet);
						// 20200921 수정
						data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, searchParamPageSize, '', ''
								, '', '', '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
								, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet);

						that.getTabContents(sort, data);
						return;
					}

					var minPrice = searchResultManager.minPrice
							, maxPrice = searchResultManager.maxPrice;

					if ( !searchResultManager.isSliderClicked ) {
						minPrice = '';
						maxPrice = '';
					}

// 							data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, that.searchConstant['TAB'].PAGESIZE, '', ''
// 										, maxPrice, minPrice, '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
// 										, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet);
					// 20200921 수정
					data = new WNSearchParamVo(that.getKeyword(), 0, that.searchConstant.COLLECTION_NAME, sort, searchParamPageSize, '', ''
							, maxPrice, minPrice, '', '', '', exQuery, 'b2c', that.isMobileYN, that.isBestMatchYn, that.suggestion
							, that.isFilterSet, that.isFilter1stSet, that.isFilter2ndSet);

					pager.currentPage        = currentPage;
					pager.data.isBestMatchYn = that.isBestMatchYn;
					pager.data.exQuery       = exQuery;
					pager.data.sort          = sort;
					pager.data.minPrice      = minPrice;
					pager.data.maxPrice      = maxPrice;
					pager.getPage(currentPage);

					that.getFilterMobileTabContents(data);
				},

				// 전체 Tab에서 정렬 변경
				sortingAllResult: function(e) {
					var $target        = $(e.target)
							, $parent        = $target.parent()
							, sort           = $target.attr('sort')
							, that           = searchResultManager
							, $ul            = $target.closest('ul')
							, collectionName = $ul.attr('collection-name');

					that.searchConstant = searchConstants[collectionName];

					if ( $parent.hasClass('tab') ) {
						that.getAllSortedContents(sort);
					}
					if ( $parent.hasClass('sub-tab') ) {
						var callback = '';
						if ( collectionName == searchConstants.service.COLLECTION_NAME ) {
							callback = that.eventListener.setServiceContents;
						}
						if ( collectionName == searchConstants.digitalPlaza.COLLECTION_NAME ) {
							callback = that.eventListener.setDigitalPlazaContents;
						}

						that.getAllSortedMultiContents(collectionName, sort, callback);
					}
				},

				// 전체 정렬 변경 시 고객서비스 callback
				setServiceContents: function(result) {
					var $manual = $(result).find('#manual').children();
					var $notice = $(result).find('#notice').children();

					$('#tabContentAll ul.list-type-download').empty();
					$('#tabContentAll div.list-type-notice').empty();
					$('#tabContentAll ul.list-type-download').append($manual);
					$('#tabContentAll div.list-type-notice').append($notice);
				},
				// 전체 정렬 변경 시 디지털프라자 callback
				setDigitalPlazaContents: function(result) {
					var $event = $(result).find('#plazaEvent').children();
					var $base  = $(result).find('#plazaBase').children();

					$('#tabContentAll ul.list-type-exhibition.plaza-event').empty();
					$('#tabContentAll ul.list-type-store').empty();
					$('#tabContentAll ul.list-type-exhibition.plaza-event').append($event);
					$('#tabContentAll ul.list-type-store').append($base);
				},
				/* e: Tab 정렬 이벤트 */

				/* s: filter */
				// URL에 값이 설정되어 들어온 경우
				getExQueryWhenTabTriggered: function(collectionName, exQuery) {
					var exQueryText = ''
							, regExp = ''
							, exQueryList;

					if ( collectionName == 'product' ) {
						regExp = /(.*?=\w+)(\%2B|\%7C)*/g;
					} else {
						regExp = /(.*?\w+)(\%2B|\%7C)*/g;
					}

					while( exQueryList = regExp.exec(exQuery) ) {
						exQueryText += exQueryList[1];
					}

					return exQueryText;
				},

				filterAppendingHtml: function(filterType, filterValue, text, classType) {
					return '<li class="item filter-footeritem ' + classType + '" filter-type="' + filterType + '" target-value="' + filterValue + '">'
							+ '<span class="txt">' + text + '</span>'
							+ '<button type="text" class="btn-delete">닫기</button>'
							+ '</li>';
				},
				getExcludedFilterNameList: function() {
					var that                   = searchResultManager
							, $fixedFilter           = $('div.btn-filter-depth1.fixed')
							, excludedFilterNameList = [];

					$.each($fixedFilter, function(idx, element) {
						var filterName = $(element).attr('filter-name');
						if ( filterName != undefined ) {
							excludedFilterNameList.push(filterName);
						}
					});

					return excludedFilterNameList;
				},

				// 필터 삭제(collection이 product가 아닌 경우)
				deleteBtnFilter: function(e, collectionName) {
					var that        = searchResultManager
							, $target       = $(e.target)
							, $li           = $target.parent()
							, filterType    = $li.attr('filter-type')
							, filterValue   = $li.attr('target-value')
							, $filterTarget = $('.filter-cont ul[filter-type="' + filterType + '"] input[code="' + filterValue + '"');

					$li.remove();
					$filterTarget.prop('checked', false);
					$filterTarget.removeAttr('selected');

					that.isFilterSelected = undefined;
					that.removeFilterQuery(filterValue);

					if ( $('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] li').length == 0 ) {
						$('.btn-filter-reset').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
					}
					$($('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li')[0]).trigger('click');
				},

				// 필터 삭제(collection이 product인 경우)
				deleteProductBtnFilter: function(e) {
					var that         = searchResultManager
							, $target        = $(e.target)
							, $li            = $target.parent()
							, filterType     = $li.attr('filter-type')
							, filterValue    = $li.attr('target-value')
							, $filterTarget  = $('.filter-cont ul[filter-type="' + filterType + '"] input[code="' + filterValue + '"')
							, filterName     = $('.filter-cont ul[filter-type="' + filterType + '"]').attr('filter-name')
							, $filterDiv     = $('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName +'"]')
							, collectionName = 'product';

					$li.remove();
					$filterTarget.prop('checked', false);
					$filterTarget.removeAttr('selected');
					that.isFilterSelected = undefined;

					if ( $('.filter-footer[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"] li').length == 0 ) {
						$filterDiv.removeAttr('selected');
						$('.btn-filter-reset').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
					}
					var key = '';

					// 카테고리 1Depth
					if ( filterType == 'category' ) {
						that.eventListener.initFilterByCategory();
						$('.btn-filter-reset').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
						$($('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li')[0]).trigger('click');
						return;

						// 카테고리 2Depth
					} else if ( filterType == 'check' ) {
						$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].fluid').removeAttr('selected');
						key = searchConstants.filter.product.CATEGORY_M;

						/* 2Depth가 선택되지 않은 경우, 하위 필터 모두 삭제 */
						if ( $('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li[filter-type="' + filterType + '"]').length == 0 ) {
							that.isFilter1stSet = undefined;

							$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].fluid').hide();
							$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].fluid input').prop('checked', false);
							$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].fluid input').removeAttr('selected');
							$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li.fluid').remove();

						} else {
							that.isFilter1stSet = 'Y';
						}

						// 그외 filter
					} else {
						if ( $('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li[filter-type="' + filterType + '"]').length == 0 ) {
							$filterDiv.removeAttr('selected');
						}

						key = filterName;
					}

					that.removeFilterProductQuery(key, filterName + ':' + filterValue);
					$($('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li')[0]).trigger('click');
				},

				// Product 카테고리 필터 초기화
				initFilterByCategory: function() {
					var that = searchResultManager;

					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] div.fluid').hide();
					$('.filter-cont .category-depth2').hide();
					$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"][filter-type="category"]').remove();
					$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] ul').empty();
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .category-depth2 input').prop('checked', false);
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .category-depth2 input').removeAttr('selected');
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.fluid input').prop('checked', false);
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.fluid input').removeAttr('selected');
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.fixed input').prop('checked', false);
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.fixed input').removeAttr('selected');
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.changeable input').prop('checked', false);
					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.changeable input').removeAttr('selected');

					$('.result-filter-wrap[collection-name="product"] .btn-filter-depth1.changeable').removeAttr('selected');

					that.eventListener.initPriceSlider();
					that.filterProductQuery      = undefined;
					that.isFilter1stSet          = undefined;
					that.minPrice                = '';
					that.maxPrice                = '';
					that.isSliderClicked         = false;
					that.isSliderClickedForEvent = false;
				},
				isCategoryNotSelected: function() {
					var that = searchResultManager;

					if ( $('.category-filter input:checked').length == 0 ) {
						that.isCategoryNotSelected = true;
						return;
					}
					that.isCategoryNotSelected = false;
				},
				// 제품 카테고리 1Depth 필터 선택
				filterProductSearch1Depth: function(e) {
					var that                    = searchResultManager
							, $target                 = $(e.target)
							, $filterUl               = $target.parent().parent()
							, filterType              = $filterUl.attr('filter-type')
							, filterName              = $filterUl.attr('filter-name')
							, filterValue             = $target.attr('code')
							, appendingText           = $target.next().text()
							, isChecked               = $target.attr('checked')
							, $filterFooterList       = $('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li[filter-type="' + filterType + '"]')
							, filterFooterFilterValue = $filterFooterList.attr('target-value')
							, collectionName          = 'product';

					// 이미 선택한 category인 경우
					if ( filterValue == filterFooterFilterValue ) {
						$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li[filter-type="' + filterType + '"][target-value="' + filterValue + '"] button.btn-delete').trigger('click');
						return;
					}

					that.eventListener.initFilterByCategory();
					that.isFilter1stSet        = undefined;
					that.isFilterSelected      = true;
					that.isCategoryNotSelected = false;

					that.eventListener.setBtnResetDisabled(collectionName);
					that.setFilterProductQuery(searchConstants.filter.product.CATEGORY_L, filterName + ':' + filterValue);

					$('.filter-cont .category-depth2 li:not([code="' + filterValue + '"])').hide();
					$('.filter-cont .category-depth2 li[code="' + filterValue + '"]').show();
					$('.filter-cont .category-depth2').show();

					var $appendingTarget = $(that.eventListener.filterAppendingHtml(filterType, filterValue, appendingText, 'fixed'));
					$appendingTarget.on('click', 'button.btn-delete', function(e) {
						that.eventListener.deleteProductBtnFilter(e);
					});
					$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] ul').append($appendingTarget);

					$($('ul.droplist[collection-name="' + collectionName + '"][search-type="TAB"] li')[0]).trigger('click');
				},

				// 제품 카테고리 2Depth 필터 선택
				filterProductSearch2Depth: function(e) {
					var that              = searchResultManager
							, $target           = $(e.target)
							, $filterUl         = $target.parent().parent()
							, filterType        = $filterUl.attr('filter-type')
							, filterName        = $filterUl.attr('filter-name')
							, $filterDiv        = $('div.item[filter-name="' + filterName +'"]')
							, filterValue       = $target.attr('code')
							, appendingText     = $target.next().text()
							, isSelected        = $target.attr('selected')
							, $fixedFilter      = $('div.btn-filter-depth1.fixed');

					$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].fluid input').prop('checked', false);
					$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].fluid input').removeAttr('selected');
					$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li.fluid').remove();

					$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].changeable input').prop('checked', false);
					$('.btn-filter-depth1[collection-name="product"].changeable input').removeAttr('selected');
					$('.filter-footer[collection-name="product"] li.changeable').remove();

					that.isFilterSelected = true;
					that.removeFilterProductQueryByKey(searchConstants.filter.product.CATEGORY_L, searchConstants.filter.product.CATEGORY_M);

					if ( isSelected != undefined || isSelected ) {
						$target.removeAttr('selected');
